    *   è¦ä»¶ã¨ã—ã¦ã¯ã€Œå‹•çš„è§£æã€ã¯ Phase 3 ä»¥é™ã® **ã‚ªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚¤ãƒ³**ã€ã‹ã¤ä»£æ›¿ï¼ˆsampling profilerç­‰ï¼‰ã‚’ä½µè¨˜ã™ã‚‹ã®ãŒå¦¥å½“ï¼ˆä¾‹ï¼špy-spyï¼‰ [Real Python+2GitHub+2](https://realpython.com/python-profiling/?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

### 3.2 `api_objects`ï¼ˆAPIã‚«ã‚¿ãƒ­ã‚°ï¼šæ ¸å¿ƒï¼‰

*   `parameters_json` (string(JSON), nullable) ä¾‹: `[{name,type,default,kind}, ...]`
*   `return_annotation` (string, nullable)
*   `docstring` (string, nullable)
*   `doc_style` (category, nullable) `google/numpy/rst/unknown`
*   `source_path` (string, nullable) / `lineno` (int, nullable)
*   `extraction_method` (category, not null) `ast/libcst/runtime/griffe`
*   `errors` (string, nullable)

### 3.3 V5å†…éƒ¨ã‚ªãƒ–ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆï¼ˆUI/ç”Ÿæˆã®æœ€å°å¥‘ç´„ï¼‰

*   `CallableSpec`: signature / params(name,type,default,kind) / return\_type / doc\_summary
*   `ValueCandidate`: value / source / confidenceï¼ˆç¢ºåº¦ï¼‰
*   `models_v5.py`: ParamDefaults / ParamKinds / ParamValueHints / global\_defaultsï¼ˆåŒåå¼•æ•°ã®é›†è¨ˆï¼‰

### 3.4 é¡ä¼¼ãƒ»ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ãƒ»ã‚¯ãƒ©ã‚¹ã‚¿ï¼ˆæ‹¡å¼µãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ï¼‰

*   `similarity_edges`: seedâ†’candidate ã® `score` ã¨èª¬æ˜æ ¹æ‹ ï¼ˆä¸Šä½ç‰¹å¾´ï¼‰ã‚’ä¿æŒï¼ˆGraphã®å…¥åŠ›ï¼‰
*   `clusters`: `cluster_id/size/representative/keywords/label`ï¼ˆäººæ‰‹ã§ãƒ©ãƒ™ãƒ«ä»˜ã‘å¯èƒ½ï¼‰

### âœ… Codeã‚»ãƒ« 2ï¼ˆpip list å–å¾—â†’å°å¸³åŒ–â†’ä¿å­˜ï¼‰

```python
import subprocess
import sys as _sys
from lib_ana.io_piplist import parse_pip_list_columns
from lib_ana.cache_store import CacheStore

snapshot_id = "snapshot_demo"

text = subprocess.check_output([_sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "list"], text=True)
res = parse_pip_list_columns(text, snapshot_id=snapshot_id)

store = CacheStore(paths.cache)
store.write_text(text, name="pip_list", snapshot_id=snapshot_id, ext="txt")
inv_path = store.write_df(res.df, name="packages_inventory", snapshot_id=snapshot_id)

print("parse errors:", res.errors)
print("saved:", inv_path)
res.df.head(10)
```
